=== SEARCH SNIPPETS ===

[Salem Prize - Wikipedia]
The Salem Prize, in memory of Raphael Salem, is awarded each year to young researchers for outstanding contributions to the field of analysis. It is awarded by the School of Mathematics at the Institute for Advanced Study in Princeton and was founded by the widow of Raphael Salem in his memory. The prize is considered highly prestigious and many Fields Medalists previously received it.
URL: https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Salem_Prize

=== FULL EXTRACTED CONTENT ===


--- [Salem Prize - Wikipedia] ---
The Salem Prize, in memory of Raphael Salem, is awarded each year to young researchers for outstanding contributions to the field of analysis. It is awarded by the School of Mathematics at the Institute for Advanced Study in Princeton and was founded by the widow of Raphael Salem in his memory. The prize is considered highly prestigious and many Fields Medalists previously received it. The prize was 5000 French Francs in 1990.


--- [Previous Salem Prize Winners - Institute for Advanced Study] ---
Previous Salem Prize Winners Previous Salem Prize Winners Previous Salem Prize Winners (listed in ascending order) - 1968 - Nicolas Th. Varopoulos - 1969 - Richard Hunt - 1970 - Yves Meyer - 1971 - Charles Fefferman - 1972 - Thomas Körner - 1973 - E.M. Nikishin - 1974 - Hugh Montgomery - 1975 - William Beckner - 1976 - Michaël R. Herman - 1977 - S. V. Bockarev - 1978 - Björn E. Dahlberg - 1979 - Gilles Pisier - 1980 - Stylianos Pichorides - 1981 - Peter Jones - 1982 - Alexei B. Aleksandrov - 1983 - Jean Bourgain - 1984 - Carlos Kenig - 1985 - Thomas H. Wolff - 1986 - Nikolai. G. Makarov - 1987 - Guy David and Jean-Lin Journé - 1988 - Alexander Volberg and Jean-Christophe Yoccoz - 1990 - Sergei Vladimirovich Konyagin - 1991 - Curt McMullen - 1992 - Mitsuo Shishikura - 1993 - Sergei Treil - 1994 - Kari Astala - 1995 - Håkan Eliasson - 1996 - Michael Lacey and Christoph Thiele - 1998 - Trevor Wooley - 1999 - Fedor Nazarov2003- Elon Lindenstrauss and Kannan Soundararajan - 2000- Terence Tao - 2001- Oded Schramm and Stanislav Smirnov - 2002- Xavier Tolsa - 2003- Elon Lindenstrauss and Kannan Soundararajan * Years not listed did not have a selected winner


--- [2025 Salem Prize Winners | School of Mathematics | Institute for Advanced Study] ---
2025 Salem Prize Winners 2025 Salem Prize Announcement The 2025 Salem Prize is awarded separately to Vesselin Dimitrov and Hong Wang. Vesselin Dimitrov is awarded the Salem prize for fundamental contributions to Diophantine geometry and number theory. Hong Wang is awarded the Salem prize for her role in solutions to major open problems in harmonic analysis and geometric measure theory.
